PAGE 1: History Worth Exploring - Old Royal Naval College

URL: https://ornc.org/

HEADINGS: Celebrating 300 Years of the Painted Hall, Welcome to the Old Royal Naval College, an extraordinary cultural destination in the heart of the Maritime Greenwich UNESCO World Heritage Site., Mother's Day Afternoon Tea, What's On in 2026, SUPPORT THE OLD ROYAL NAVAL COLLEGE, Getting Here, Book Now, Opening Times, Getting Here, Book Now, Opening Times, What's on, Regency Mother’s Day Afternoon Tea, Greenwich Dog Show 2026, Murder Mystery Experience

CONTENT:
Celebrating 300 Years of the Painted Hall

Celebrate the mother figure in your life, with this Regency inspired Afternoon Tea in Admiral's House.

A year of celebration, culture, wellbeing and wonder awaits at the Old Royal Naval College, as we celebrate 300 years of the Painted Hall.

Public support is vital. While the Old Royal Naval College remains open, beautiful and thriving, maintaining it is no easy task.Please consider making a one-off or regular donation to conserve the stories, buildings, collections that make this place so special.

We’re in the heart of the Maritime Greenwich UNESCO World Heritage site. Just eight minutes on the train from London Bridge.How to get here

Purchase a General Admission ticket to the Painted Hall for £17.50. Convert it to an Annual Pass for no extra cost to give you unlimited entry for a whole year. Kids go free.

Book now

The Painted Hall, Chapel and Visitor Centre are open daily, 10am–5pm.

The grounds are open daily 8am–11pm.

Opening times

PAGE 2: Explore what's here - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/explore-whats-here/

HEADINGS: Explore what’s here, Explore what’s here, Painted Hall, 100 years of film and TV history, Discover Greenwich Museum, Skittle Alley, Chapel of St Peter & St Paul, Nelson Room, Greenwich Palace Remains, Daily Talks and Tours, Plan a visit, How to get here, Talks and tours

CONTENT:
Travel through 600 years of extraordinary history with our expert guides, experience the magnificence of the Painted Hall and wander among some of Britain’s finest Baroque buildings in the UNESCO World Heritage site.

These are just some of the wonderful things to do and see when you visit the Old Royal Naval College in Greenwich. You can buy your ticketsonlineor in person at the Visitor Centre.

Visit our award-winning Painted Hall and discover more about the 200 characters on the ceiling.

We’re celebrating 100 years of film and TV with a new tour, special events, behind-the-scenes content and more.

Start your visit here and explore Greenwich's fascinating history through captivating artifacts and interactive exhibits in our newly renovated museum space.

No visit is complete without a roll of the wooden bowling balls at the Skittle Alley. The Victorian Skittle Alley (or Bowling Alley) was installed in 1873, the inaugural year of the Royal Naval College, for the use of officers in training and is still in action for visitors to play today.Open daily 12pm – 3pm

With its richly decorated ceiling, naval themes, and exceptional altarpiece painted by ‘the Raphael of America’, Benjamin West, it is evident why the Chapel is now regarded as one of the finest neo-classical interiors in existence. The Chapel is open daily to all, regardless of tradition or background.

Visit the location where Lord Nelson's body lay in state after the Battle of Trafalgar.

Catch a glimpse of the remnants of Greenwich Palace, a place of great significance, as it was the birthplace of Henry VIII, Elizabeth I, and Mary I.

These are included in the price of your ticket.







Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

© 2025 Old Royal Naval College. All rights reserved.

PAGE 3: Film & TV location - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/explore-whats-here/filming-location/

HEADINGS: Film & TV location, Explore what's here, Celebrating 100 Years of Film with a Guinness World Records™ Award, Step behind the scenes with our new film tour, UK's #1 filming heritage location, Greenwich: A key destination for set-jetters, Secret star of Bridgerton, Perfect backdrop for your next production, Every film supports our heritage, Film Tour: Wigs, Weddings, Powder and Palaces, Regency Afternoon Tea on the Colonnades, Afternoon Teas

CONTENT:
Ever wondered how historic landmarks become film and TV stars? Over the past 100 years, our site has featured in more than300 productions, making us the UK’s most filmed heritage location.

To celebrate 100 years of filming at the Old Royal Naval College, we’ve launched abrand‑new tourand a year packed full of events.

Step behind the scenes and discover how our historic site brings stories to life on screen. Make the most of your day in Greenwich create your own movie moment.



The Old Royal Naval College and Elstree Studios have made history setting an official Guinness World Records™ Award for the largest gathering of people dressed as film and TV characters - with 874 people dressed as screen characters flocking to the UNESCO World Heritage Site in celebration of filmmaking.

From period dramas to action blockbusters, the Old Royal Naval College has starred in some of the world’s biggest productions. Now you can follow in the footsteps of your favourite characters with our brand new Film & TV Tour, exploring the iconic spots seen in Bridgerton, The Crown, Les Misérables and more.

This historic site has played host to some of the biggest names in film and television. Whether it’s transforming into revolutionary Paris, Victorian London, or a dystopian future, the Old Royal Naval College adapts effortlessly across genres and eras. From Netflix hits like Bridgerton and The Crown to a host of blockbuster films, check out the extensive list of blockbuster films and TV shows filmed at the Old Royal Naval College.

Set-jetting is on the rise!VisitBritain’s #StarringGREATBritain campaign is celebrating the UK’s standout film and TV locations - including ours!Visit Greenwich's campaign 'Unmissable Greenwich' reimagines the borough as the ultimate film set, inviting you to create your own movie moment.

Walking through the Old Royal Naval College grounds feels like stepping back in time, so it should come as no surprise that this historical site has been used as a dramatic backdrop to bring to life the fashion and glamour of the Regency era in every season of Bridgerton.

We can accommodate a wide range of filming and photography requests including:Documentary and commercial filmingPersonal and commercial photographyWedding photographyNews and media.

Filming here does more than dazzle audiences - it helps protect our heritage. Location fees at the Old Royal Naval College go directly towards preserving this majestic landmark for future generations to enjoy, both onscreen and in person.

Step into the world of period drama and experience the UK’s most filmed heritage site like never before.

Step into the world of period drama and experience the UK’s most filmed heritage site like never before.

Be transported back to Regency-era London with a Bridgerton-inspired afternoon tea offer.

Be transported back to Regency-era London with a Bridgerton-inspired afternoon tea offer.

Celebrate 100 years of film and TV, with a movie-inspired afternoon tea experience in the UK’s most filmed heritage location.

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

================================================================================
PAGE 4: Talks and tours - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/plan-a-visit/talks-and-tours/

HEADINGS: Talks and tours, Plan a visit, Painted Hall Talks, Official tour: 600 Years of History Tour, Lie back, look up, and let the stories unfold with a multimedia guide, Film Tour | Wigs, Weddings, Powder and Palaces, Secret Dome Tour, Private tours, Discover our free digital guide, Access tours, Plan your visit, Plan a visit, Explore what’s here, How to get here

CONTENT:
Whether you’re a first-time visitor or returning to explore deeper, no two visits are ever the same thanks to our expert guides who bring the site to life with fascinating insights, hidden details and stories you won’t find in the guidebook.

From royal connections and naval heroes to blockbuster filming secrets, each tour uncovers a new layer of this iconic riverside landmark. Come curious, leave inspired!

Included in your General Admission ticket

Join our expert guides and meet the cast of over 200 vibrant characters brought to life in Sir James Thornhill’s Painted Hall masterpiece. Uncover the rich history, hidden meanings and epic tales behind a work that took 19 years to complete.

Daily | Every 30 mins from 11am – 4pm.

Learn more

Included in your General Admission ticket

From our early years as a Tudor Place, to the masterpiece you see today built by Sir Christopher Wren, dive into the history and architecture of this iconic site.

Daily | 11am, 12pm, 1pm, 2pm, 3pm

Learn more

Included in your General Admission ticket

Discover the Painted Hall in a whole new way with our multimedia guide. Perfect for exploring at your own pace, it’s packed with fascinating insights to help you get the most out of your visit.

Available in seven languages – English, French, Spanish, German, Italian, Japanese, Mandarin and British Sign Language – and free to use. Just ask a member of staff and get ready to uncover the secrets of this spectacular space.

Whether you’re a film buff, history lover, or just curious to see where some of your favourite scenes were shot, join this unforgettable experience to celebrate 100 years of film and TV. Step into the spotlight, learn Bridgerton fan etiquette and experience Britain’s most filmed heritage site like never before.

Fridays & Saturdays | 1.30pm & 3.30pm

Book now

Join us for an exclusive adventure into Wren’s Dome. Only six people at a time will be able to see and hear about the creation of this remarkable building from an expert guide, unravelling secrets of the space rarely open to the public.

Book now

Enjoy a more personal experience of one of London’s most iconic landmarks with a private guided tour.

Led by our award-winning expert guides, private tours are perfect for individuals, couples or small groups looking to explore at their own pace. Choose from our range of themed tours covering everything from art and architecture to naval history and film.

Looking for something specific? Let us know – we may be able to tailor your tour to suit your interests.

Enhance your visit or explore the Old Royal Naval College from anywhere in the world with our digital guide, available as part of the free Bloomberg Connects app. Available in over 40 languages.

We deliver a range of accessible tours throughout the year.

Explore ourWhat’s Onpage to find out more.







Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

PAGE 5: Painted Hall - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/explore-whats-here/painted-hall/

HEADINGS: Painted Hall, Explore what's here, Visiting the Painted Hall, Visiting with children, What do the paintings mean?, The Painted Hall Through Time, Who was Sir James Thornhill?

CONTENT:


People’s reaction when they see the Painted Hall for the first time is something to behold. Designed bySir James Thornhill and painted between1707 and 1726,the Painted Hall features more than 3,700 square metres of Baroque walls and ceilings. These surfaces are covered in striking images depicting 200 figures including kings, queens and mythological creatures.

Itwas originally intended as an eating space for theGreenwich Pensionerswho lived at theRoyal Hospital, as it was called then, but it soon became a tourist attraction and was used for dining only on special occasions.

The Painted Hall reopened in 2019, following a two year long, award-winning conservation project and is now open for visits, tours and to hire.

Experience ‘Britain’s Sistine Chapel’ and discover a truly extraordinary space. Multimedia guides (available in seven languages) are available included in your ticket price.  Regular talks about the history and meaning of the Painted Hall take place every half hour from 11am to 4pm.

Find out more

Children are welcome at the Painted Hall. Kids aged 16 or under go free (up to four children per paying adult). A free activity booklet is available as well Explorer Backpacks filled with sensory objects to borrow for little ones.



Sir James Thornhill’s epic painting draws on a cast of around 200 figures to tell an incredible story of political change, scientific and cultural achievements, naval endeavours and commercial enterprise all set against a series of magnificent backdrops. The characters he included are a mix of allegorical, mythological, historical and contemporary.

The central narrative focuses on a pivotal moment when the United Kingdom was created and became a dominant power in Europe. The paintings celebrate Britain’s political stability, commercial prosperity and naval power. It also depicts the Protestant accessions to the throne of King William III and Queen Mary II in 1688 and George I in 1714.

Explore our Virtual Tour tool to learn more

The Painted Hall was once a dining hall for Greenwich Pensioners and Naval Officers, as well as aNaval Art Gallery. Perhaps the most significant function was the lying-in-state of Lord Nelson in 1806, ahead of his funeral in central London. More recently, it has become a dramatic backdrop in popular films and TV shows.

The National Gallery of Naval Art, from a postcard sent in 1924.

Sir James Thornhill (1675-1734) was an English painter of historical events working in an Italian Baroque style.

He spent 19 years planning and painting the magnificent Painted Hall and was well rewarded for his efforts. He was paid one pound for every yard – about a square metre – on the walls andthreepounds for the same on the ceiling. That came to a total of £6,685 – about £1.4 million in today’s money.

He was also the first English artist to be knighted in 1720 by George I.

Find out more

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

© 2025 Old Royal Naval College. All rights reserved.

PAGE 7: Our History - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/our-history/

HEADINGS: Our History, Our History, Greenwich Palace (1498 – 1694), Royal Hospital for Seamen (1694 – 1869), Royal Naval College (1873 – 1997), The Greenwich Foundation (1998 – today)

CONTENT:
This iconic riverside estate boasts 600 years of rich history linking an incredible cast of monarchs and famous British figures includingKing Henry VIII, Queen Elizabeth I,William Shakespeare, King William andQueen Mary Iand Vice-Admiral Lord Nelson.

Built on the site of the Palace of Placentia, also known asGreenwich Palace, this extraordinary building, designed by esteemed architect Sir Christopher Wren, has seen life as both aRoyal Hospitaland aRoyal Naval College. From Henry VIII’s birthplace toLord Nelson’slying in state, these walls contain a wealth of key historical moments.

Become one of the 1.2m annual visitors exploring Greenwich. Drop into theVisitor Centreto understand the many layered histories of these grounds, visit the iconicPainted Hall, known as the ‘UK’s Sistine Chapel’ or spend time in theSt Peter & St Paul Chapelto find out why it is considered to be one of the finest 18th century interiors in existence.

Welcome to Greenwich Palace, one of the great royal houses of Tudor England. What is today a calm, picturesque site haswitnessedcenturies of turmoil, births, deaths,marriagesand much physical change. There are many fascinating stories to tell.

The Royal Hospital for Seamen is one of the world’s great architectural treasures. Founded by Queen Mary II and designed by Sir Christopher Wren, the Hospital was created to provide a refuge for elderly and injured Royal Navyseamen.

This ‘University of the Navy’ taught officers the seamanship skills needed for an era when steam power was replacing sail. It quickly became the most highly rated naval officers’ training college in Europe, earning a reputation for academic rigour.

For 25 years The Greenwich Foundation has conserved the magnificent baroque buildings and grounds of the Old Royal Naval College for present and future generations.

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

© 2025 Old Royal Naval College. All rights reserved.

================================================================================
PAGE 9: Make a donation - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/support-us/make-a-donation/

HEADINGS: Make a donation, Support us, Education, Conservation, Painted Hall Project, Donate today, Other ways to support us, Leave a legacy, Become a Patron

CONTENT:
Each year, we carry out over 10,000 hours of conservation work, host over 15,500 learners, and welcome over 800,000 visitors to our buildings and grounds.Every donation, no matter the size, counts to help support this important work.

Please use the link below to donate now orset up a monthly donation. To learn more, please contact us by email atdevelopment@ornc.org







We aim to inspire and engage schools and other community groups in our heritage and creativity. Support from our donors helps us to fund our education work.

Learn more about how we are empoweringEnglish language learners through heritage and creativityandsupporting creative learning for children in hospital.

Conserving our grounds and buildings is central to our charitable mission. Thanks to the generosity of our supporters, we are carrying out essential works to maintain and bring elements of our site back to life.

Learn more about our conservation of theChapel organand the cleaning of theFour Graces statues.

An £8.5m restoration to clean and conserve Sir James Thornhill’s epic Baroque interiors was completed in 2019. Thanks to our donors and partners, the Painted Hall has been brought vividly back to life and is now open to the public.

The project has won a number of awards, including a prestigious Museums & Heritage Award for Restoration/Conservation project of the Year and two RIBA awards.

Donations provide us with vital support to help preserve, protect, and interpret our site for the future.

Please consider leaving a gift to the Old Royal Naval College in your will.

Our generous Patrons provide invaluable support to our conservation and education projects.

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

© 2025 Old Royal Naval College. All rights reserved.

================================================================================
PAGE 10: Support us - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/support-us/

HEADINGS: Support us, Support us, Make a donation, Become a Patron, Leave a legacy, American Friends

CONTENT:
Described by UNESCO as being of ‘outstanding universal value’, the Old Royal Naval College is the architectural centrepiece of the Maritime Greenwich World Heritage Site. Boasting600 years of rich history,it is a gem we must preserve for future generations to experience and enjoy.

Our award-winning £8.5 million Painted Hall conservation project is the template for our future ambitions to conserve and protect this historic site and unlock more of the Old Royal Naval College’s hidden spaces.

As a registered charity we rely on funding from charitable trusts, donors, Patrons and Members and those who generously choose to leave a legacy to support our work. Find out how you can support us.

By making a donation you will help safeguard the Old Royal Naval College for future generations.

Our generous Patrons provide invaluable support to our conservation and education projects.

Please consider leaving a gift to the Old Royal Naval College in your will.

The American public can support us through the American Friends of the Old Royal Naval College (AFORNC)

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

© 2025 Old Royal Naval College. All rights reserved.

PAGE 11: Plan a visit - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/plan-a-visit/

HEADINGS: Plan a visit, Getting Here, Book Now, Opening Times, Getting Here, Book Now, Opening Times, Plan a visit, , Explore what's here, Getting to Greenwich, Opening times and closures, Discover our free digital guide, Talks and tours, Accessibility, Family visits, Eating and drinking, Shopping, Photography & filming guidelines, Pay once, visit all year, What can I see for free?, Group and coach visits

CONTENT:
We’re in the heart of the Maritime Greenwich UNESCO World Heritage site. Just eight minutes on the train from London Bridge.How to get here

Purchase a General Admission ticket to the Painted Hall for £17.50. Convert it to an Annual Pass for no extra cost to give you unlimited entry for a whole year. Kids go free.

Book now

The Painted Hall, Chapel and Visitor Centre are open daily, 10am–5pm.

The grounds are open daily 8am–11pm.

Opening times

We’re in the heart of the Maritime Greenwich UNESCO World Heritage site. Just eight minutes on the train from London Bridge.How to get here

Purchase a General Admission ticket to the Painted Hall for £17.50. Convert it to an Annual Pass for no extra cost to give you unlimited entry for a whole year. Kids go free.

Book now

The Painted Hall, Chapel and Visitor Centre are open daily, 10am–5pm.

The grounds are open daily 8am–11pm.

Opening times

Uncover the secrets of the Painted Hall with an expert talk or multimedia guide (available in eight languages, including British Sign Language). Take a guided tour, enjoy free family activities, try your hand at the Skittle Alley, dive into local history in the Discover Greenwich museum and more.

Pay once, gain year round access to the Painted Hall, tours and captivating exhibitions for no extra cost by converting your ticket into anAnnual Pass.

ConcessionsProof of eligibility may be required

FreeProof of eligibility may be required

Find out more about what you can see and do during your visit.

Located right beside the River Thames in London, we’re a short journey away from the centre of the City and very easy to reach by tube, train, bus, boat or bike. Our Visitor Centre is only a couple of minutes’ walk from the pier or DLR station and directly opposite the famous ship, The Cutty Sark.

Explore opening times, tour dates and closures.

Enhance your visit or explore the Old Royal Naval College from anywhere with our digital guide, available as part of the free Bloomberg Connects app. Available in over 40 languages.

Our expert guides bring the site to life with fascinating insights, hidden details and stories you won’t find in the guidebook.

We welcome visitors with disabilities, their families, friends and carers.

The Old Royal Naval College is the perfect destination for families. There is plenty to discover through regular events and activities both inside the beautiful buildings and around the grounds.

Whether you wish to enjoy a leisurely lunch in the Undercroft Café, a pint with your lunch in The Old Brewery pub or a splendid afternoon tea, we have a range of food and drink options for you to choose from. Look out for our seasonal coffee, snacks and ice-cream pop-up stalls across our grounds and regular weekend food markets.

The Old Royal Naval College is home to three shops each catering to different tastes and needs, so whether you’re looking for souvenirs of your trip, gifts for a loved one, or simply to browse for books or cards, we have you covered.All purchases made in our shops make a vital contribution toward protecting our heritage for the future.

We are keen for our visitors to enjoy their experience on our site and understand that taking and sharing of photographs can be a large part of that experience.

Convert your Painted Hall ticket into an Annual Pass at no extra cost, granting you free access to all that the Old Royal Naval College has to offer for 12 months including the Painted Hall, exhibitions, tours, Discover Greenwich and more.

Our extensive riverside grounds are open daily for you to explore. They are a perfect place to relax, stroll, or have a picnic, surrounded by some of the finest buildings in the world. You can also visit the Chapel of St Peter & St Paul to admire the neoclassical interiors, to listen to the Monday Evensong, or to attend a Chapel Service.

We welcome groups of any size and have a range of special offers, tours and experiences to suit all interests and budgets.

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

© 2025 Old Royal Naval College. All rights reserved.

================================================================================
PAGE 12: How to get here - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/plan-a-visit/getting-here/

HEADINGS: How to get here, Plan a visit, By DLR and Underground (Tube), By bus, By boat, Cycling and walking, By car, Accessibility, By train

CONTENT:
Download our site map

Getting here while Cutty Sark Station is closed

From 31 May 2025,Cutty Sark Station will be temporarily closedfor renovations. But don’t worry – there are plenty of easy ways to reach us!

Hop off the DLR at Island Gardens (just a 10-minute walk), Greenwich Station (11 minutes and step-free), take one of the local bus services, or enjoy a scenic ride on the Uber Boat by Thames Clipper.

The DLR connects with other Underground lines at Bank, Canary Wharf, TowerGatewayand Stratford stations.

We strongly recommend checkingTransport for London(TfL)before you leave for any travel updates.

Alternative option

Take the Jubilee line to North Greenwich Station then get the 188 bus or river boat one stop to Greenwich Pier.

Bus routes 129, 177, 188,199, 286 and 386are a short walking distance.

We strongly recommend checkingTransport for London(TfL)before you leave for any travel updates.

Start your visit in maritimestyle with a boat trip to Greenwich Pier, just moments from the Old Royal Naval College.

Uber Boat by Thames ClippersFast and frequent services run every 20minutes from central Londonincluding LondonEye Pier(45 mins), London Bridge Pier (25 mins) and Tower Pier (20 mins).

Plan your journey

Sightseeing cruisesCity CruisesandThames River Sightseeingoffer regular trips to and from Greenwich, with live commentary andgreat viewsof London’s riverside landmarks.

AccessibilityGreenwich Pier has Europe’s first Ramp Rider, making it easier for wheelchair users to board at all tide levels.

TheThames Pathis a scenic walking route that follows the River Thames through London. At Greenwich, it runs along the north bank, but you can cross to the south via theGreenwich Foot Tunnel, which brings you out right by our Visitor Centre.

Greenwich is also well connected to the National CycleNetwork,andcan be reachedbytraffic-free routes. The cycle path runs from Lewin Gate at Cutty Sark Gardens to Trafalgar Gate at Park Row, with bike racks available outside the Visitor Centre and The Old Brewery.

Ifyou’replanning to visit by car, please be aware that wedon’tofferparking facilities, except for visitors with access requirements.Car parking for blue badge holders is available in the Park Row car park, opposite the East Gate entrance.

Theis limited parking in Greenwich,and we encourage you to use public transportwheneverpossible. Paid car parking is available in Park Row (SE10 9NL) and Cutty Sark Gardens.Find a public car parkin the Royal Borough of Greenwich and view information about parking spaces available.

We’recommitted to making the Old Royal Naval College welcoming and accessible to all. You can find more information on ouraccessibility page, and if you have specific questions or need support with your visit,pleaseemail us ataccess@ornc.org.

For the latest updates on accessible travel to Greenwich by train or bus, visit theTransport for London (TfL) website.

The nearest railstations areGreenwich (11minwalk)andMaze Hill (15minwalk).

These stations are served bySoutheasternandThameslinktrain lines, offering connections from various parts of London and beyond, including direct trainsfrom London Cannon Street and London Bridge.

We strongly recommend checkingNational Railbefore you leave for any travel updates.



Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

© 2025 Old Royal Naval College. All rights reserved.

================================================================================
PAGE 13: Accessibility - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/plan-a-visit/accessibility/

HEADINGS: Accessibility, Plan a visit, Access update, British Sign Language (BSL) introduction to the Old Royal Naval College, Site map, Tickets for companions and carers, Painted Hall & Nelson Room, Visitor Centre, Chapel of St Peter & St Paul, The Old Brewery, Toilets, Distances, Accessible parking, Wheelchairs, Support for neurodiverse visitors, Visual guide, Quiet and busy times to visit, British Sign Language (BSL), Blind and partially sighted visitors, Hearing loops, Audio guides, Ear defenders, Assistance dogs, Lighting, Rest areas, Lift maintenance

CONTENT:
The Old Royal Naval College is a large site with historic, Grade I listed buildings. We’ve made as much of the site as accessible as possible, and our team is always happy to help you find the easiest routes based on what you’d like to explore.

The lifts into the Painted Hall are currently out of order. There are 7 steps to access the King William Undercroft, 20 steps to reach the Lower Vestibule, 16 steps to the Main Vestibule, and a further 7 steps to the Upper Hall. You can also explore the Painted Hall online via ourvirtual tour.

The lift in the Visitor Centre is currently out of order. During this time, access to the exhibition area is only possible via a staircase. The staircase has 20 steps and is fitted with a fixed banister on either side. The ground floor of the Visitor Centre has full level access.

If you have specific access needs, please email boxoffice@ornc.org in advance so we can plan the best possible support for your visit.

The following video, Signs of the Past, has been created by a group of young people from DeafQuake as part of a project exploring the history of the Old Royal Naval College.

Download a transcript of the video

The dotted line on the map above shows step free access across the site. The distance from East Gate to West Gate is approximately 372 metres (1,220 feet). If you are visiting between 10am–5pm and would like assistance, please ask a member of our team.

If you require support during your visit, you’re welcome to bring a companion, carer or personal assistant at no extra cost. This applies to all ticketed areas and events across the Old Royal Naval College.There’s no need to provide proof of disability, but if you have any questions or would like to arrange access in advance, feel free to get in touch with our team at boxoffice@ornc.org or call 020 8269 4799.

Lift access to the Painted Hall is currently unavailable due to a technical fault.Step-free route: Use the dotted line on the visitor map to reach the front entrance.Steps: Once inside, there are 15 steps to the Lower Hall, 6 steps to the Upper Hall.Baby changing and toilets are located next to the King William Undercroft.Lift capacity (when operational): One wheelchair user plus companion or four standing passengers.

The Visitor Centre is fully accessible with level access on the ground floor and a lift to the mezzanine. Baby changing and accessible toilets are available here. Open daily, 10am–5pm.Access is included with a General Admission ticket or £3 Discover Greenwich ticket.

Wheelchair access to the Chapel is via a lift on College Way. Please email drobson@ornc.org in advance so we can make sure someone is available to assist.Note: The lift is not in use during services or recitals.A Stairmate is also available for access into the Chapel.Mobility scooters cannot use the lift, but a manual wheelchair is available – please email us to reserve it.Alternative route: If you can’t use the spiral staircase (19 steps), staff can direct you to a separate entrance with just two steps.

Fully level access throughout, with an accessible toilet available.

Visitor Centre: Main toilets with level access, an accessible toilet and baby changing. Open daily, 10am–5pm. Access with a General Admission or £3 Discover Greenwich ticket.Painted Hall (King William Undercroft): There is currently no step-free access due to a broken lift. Baby changing available. Open daily, 10am–5pm.The Old Brewery: Accessible toilet available.Queen Mary Undercroft (below the Chapel): Open daily, 10am–4pm (may close during events). Access via 19-step spiral staircase. If needed, speak to staff for an alternative route with two steps.

Cutty Sark to Visitor Centre - 98mGreenwich Pier to Visitor Centre - 79mVisitor Centre to Painted Hall - 245mPainted Hall to Chapel accessible entrance - 152mPainted Hall to Chapel - 48mEast Gate entrance to Painted Hall - 190mVisitor Centre to Admiral’s House - 207mAdmiral's house to Painted Hall - 118mWest Gate entrance to Painted Hall - 177mRomney Road entrance to Painted Hall - 170m

Car parking for blue badge holders is available in the Park Row car park, opposite the East Gate entrance.For taxi drop-offs, we suggest either Park Row (nearer the East Gate) or King William Walk (nearer the West Gate). The East Gate entrance is usually slightly quieter than the West Gate entrance.

Manual wheelchairs are available to hire from the Tourist Information Centre in the Visitor Centre open 10am–5pm. These are allocated on a first come, first served basis. There is a deposit of £50 which is refunded when the wheelchair is returned. For further information you can contact us by calling 020 830 55235 or emailing tic@visitgreenwich.org.uk.

We’re committed to being an accessible and welcoming site for all neurodiverse visitors, including those with autism and dementia.Many members of our Visitor Services team have received autism and dementia awareness training, including through the Alzheimer’s Society’s Dementia Friends initiative. First aid trained staff are on site daily between 10am–5pm.If you’d benefit from a guide during your visit or assistance getting to the site from Cutty Sark DLR station please call 020 8269 4799 or email access@ornc.org.

To help you prepare for your visit, we’ve created a visual guide that walks you through what to expect at the Old Royal Naval College. It includes photos and step-by-step information about key areas on site, from arriving at the entrance to exploring the Painted Hall, Chapel and Visitor Centre.This guide is especially helpful for autistic visitors, anyone with anxiety, or those who simply like to know what to expect in advance.

Our busiest times are usually in summer months, around 12–4pm. As we have a lot of outside space, the weather often has an impact on how busy the site feels. Lots of people will enjoy picnics in the grounds on a sunny day so it can be busier later into the evening. We are generally quieter before 12pm.Our quietest months are November–February. We recommend that you check our website before your visit to see if there are any special events or closures. This will have an impact on how many people are around the site.

Visitors can explore the Old Royal Naval College in British Sign Language (BSL) through our virtual tour, which includes BSL interpretation throughout. Our Painted Hall multimedia guide is also available in BSL and can be accessed on site.

An audio description of the Old Royal Naval College and its historic buildings is available on SoundCloud. This recording can help you get a sense of the site before or during your visit.

There are hearing loops installed in the Visitor Centre and the Chapel. You will see signage in places where a hearing loop is installed. If applicable to your hearing aid, please switch it to the ‘T’ position in these locations.

Audio described tours are available for blind and partially-sighted visitors. These tours are led by staff and volunteers who have been trained in audio description by Vocaleyes.

The hand dryers in our toilets are quite noisy. Ear defenders are available to borrow from the Visitor Centre, Painted Hall and Chapel. These can be used outside of the buildings but must be returned by 5pm. Please ask at our welcome desk.

Guide dogs, hearing dogs and assistance dogs are welcome in all areas of the Old Royal Naval College including the Visitor Centre, Chapel and Painted Hall.

The Visitor Centre and Chapel are both brightly lit. Light levels in the Painted Hall have to be kept lower for conservation reasons.

There are benches located across the site. Seating areas are available in the Painted Hall and the King William Undercroft below.

Please note that lift to access the Painted Hall is currently out of order due to a technical fault. There are 7 steps to access the King William Undercroft, 20 steps to access the Lower Vestibule of the Painted Hall, 16 steps to access the Main Vestibule the Painted Hall and a further 7 steps to access the Upper Hall. You can also view areas of the Painted Hall online via our virtual tour.We are committed making our site as accessible as possible for all visitors. Maintaining and repairing lifts in our historic buildings can, however, be challenging due to the nature of the repairs and the limited availability of parts for such specialist infrastructure.We recognise that this can have an enormous impact for some visitors, and we appreciate your patience and understanding. If a lift is out of order, our team is on hand to help and find solutions so you can still enjoy your visit.

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

From intimate gatherings and stylish receptions to large-scale dinners, corporate events and weddings, our beautiful and versatile spaces can be tailored to suit any occasion. Our dedicated and experienced team will work closely with you to plan and deliver a memorable event.

Located in the heart of Maritime Greenwich, a UNESCO World Heritage Site, we offer excellent transport links to Central London.

All profits from events and venue hire support the ongoing conservation and public programmes of this remarkable site.



Hire a venue with wow factor for your private event. Whether you seek grandeur or intimacy, you will find both at Sir Christopher Wren’s iconic masterpiece.

Create a marriage proposal that is as special as your love story, something you and your partner can cherish for a lifetime.

The Old Royal Naval College in Greenwich is London’s ultimate riverside wedding location, perfect at any time of year.

Our extensive riverside grounds with spectacular views offer versatile outdoor areas that are available to hire for concerts, festivals and charity events.

Explore the venue including the iconic Painted Hall, Chapel, Admiral's House, Nelson Room and Queen Mary Undercroft.

Our venue is serviced by award-winning catering and an exceptional list of recommended suppliers.

Don't just take our word for it. Read our client testimonials to find out why we are the best venue in London to host your event.

We are thrilled to have won Best Historic Venue  (over 300 attendees) and to have been shortlisted for two further awards at the prestigious 2024 London Venue & Catering Awards.

================================================================================
PAGE 16: Corporate & private events - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/venue-hire/corporate-private-events/

HEADINGS: Corporate & private events, Venue hire, Our spaces, Catering and trusted suppliers, Arrive in style, Corporate meeting hire brochure

CONTENT:
Just minutes from central London, the Old Royal Naval College is the jewel of Greenwich – and the ultimate setting for all kinds of events. Whether you seek grandeur or intimacy, you will find both at Sir Christopher Wren’s iconic masterpiece.

Set on the banks of the River Thames, Old Royal Naval College has more than its fair share of wow factor. With an imposing facade and equally impressive interior, there’s no finer private event venue in London.



With a variety of unique, characterful spaces to choose from, you’ll find the perfect place to entertain. From small gatherings to award ceremonies, weddings to outdoor drinks receptions, we can accommodate the lot.

The Old Royal Naval College is ideal for private dining events of all sizes including large gala dinners  in unforgettable surroundings.

With a bespoke menu, your guests can enjoy anything from canapés to bowl food or a three-course dinner. So, whatever you’re planning (be it large or small) the experienced event and catering team can help you bring it to life.

Arriving by boat is an excellent way to start your event, setting the tone for an occasion to impress. With the pier leading right onto the site, your event will strike the perfect note from the very beginning, as you alight to take in the stunning view. You may like to welcome your guests at the King William Colonnade for a pre-dinner drinks reception surrounded by stunning views and arresting architecture.

Explore our spaces, packages, and add-ons to create the perfect setting for meetings, conferences, and business away days.

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

© 2025 Old Royal Naval College. All rights reserved.

================================================================================
PAGE 17: Weddings - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/venue-hire/weddings/

HEADINGS: Weddings, Venue hire, Contact us, Our spaces, Catering options and trusted suppliers, Free annual pass for brides and grooms, Getting married in the Chapel, Wedding brochure - Download here, A Modern Regency

CONTENT:
One of the most spectacular and iconic landmarks in London, this elegant ensemble of buildings offers you a choice of wedding experiences, from the awe-inspiring opulence of the famousPainted Hall, to the intimate ambience of the historicAdmiral’s House.

Marrying at the Old Royal Naval College gives you exclusive permission to take photographs in the grounds with the river and fine baroque architecture as a backdrop. You can even arrive by boat to create a dramatic, one-off photo opportunity.

Click here to explore our photo gallery.



The Old Royal Naval College is breathtaking at any time of year. In the chilly days of winter the rich interiors are warm and welcoming. The classical buildings gleam and glisten in spring, and on warm summer evenings guests can enjoy an al fresco drink in the King William Colonnades. As autumn progresses, the gold, orange and russet hues of the trees add another layer of beauty to the location.

Couples who choose to marry at the Old Royal Naval College will be assigned their own wedding coordinator, supported by a team of experienced professionals who are dedicated to creating your very own fairy-tale wedding in one of the country’s most spectacular and historic places.

The famous buildings of the college that have dazzled visitors for centuries sit alongside the river with unrivalled views across to the City and Canary Wharf.

The vaulted Undercroft and the Victorian Skittle Alley can also be hired to create your own personalised wedding event, guaranteed to delight your guests and create memories to treasure for a lifetime.

Whether it’s discussing your first dance with a skilled DJ or talking bouquet ties with an expert florist – no detail is too big or too small.

You can rely on our trusted and experienced suppliers to give helpful advice and imaginative suggestions for your wedding. However, the focus is always on you – your ideas are paramount, and we will do all we can to help you bring them to life for a wedding that is as individual as you are.

We are pleased to gift our brides and grooms a free annual pass offering unlimited re-entry to the stunning Painted Hall. The pass is valid until your first wedding anniversary.

Find out about the Painted Hall

If you are interested in getting married in our iconic Chapel, which is still an active place of worship, please contact our Chapel Manager, Deborah Robson on 020 8269 4788 or emailDRobson@ornc.org.

Find out about the Chapel



Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

© 2025 Old Royal Naval College. All rights reserved.

PAGE 18: Outdoor events - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/venue-hire/outdoor-events/

HEADINGS: Outdoor events, Venue hire, Rate Guide, Contact us, UPPER AND LOWER GRAND SQUARES, King William and King Charles Lawns, Pepys Lawn, Monument Gardens and Chapel Garden, King William Courtyard and Queen Mary Courtyard, Colonnades, Dome Lighting

CONTENT:
Our extensive riverside grounds with spectacular views offer versatile outdoor areas that are available to hire forall types of events fromconcertsandfestivalstocharity events.

You can explore our outdoor spaces below or you’rewelcome toarrange a sitevisit.We’dbe delighted to show youaroundand discuss your event in person.Download our venue hire map.



Hire rates start from £1,200 ranging up to £20,000 for Upper Grand Square.

Consultation with Greenwich Foundation & Management required prior to quotation. Facility fees and security may apply.

Refundable damage deposit fee subject to the specifics of the event.

Please contact our Commercial Team on 020 8269 4798, or email us atevents@ornc.org.

One of the finest architectural and riverside views in Europe and immortalised by the Italian artist Canaletto, the Upper and Lower Grand Squares are the heart of the Maritime Greenwich UNESCO World Heritage Site.

The famous twin domes of the Old Royal Naval College, designed by Sir Christopher Wren, have appeared in multiple Hollywood blockbusters and provided an unrivalled backdrop for some incredible music festivals and live events.The domes can be lit up in colours to matchbrands or events.

The Squares comprise paved and lawn areas.

Measurements:Upper Grand Square 82m x 33mLower Grand Square 70m x 60m

Adjacent to Greenwich Pier, both the King William and King Charles Lawns are perfectly positioned for a variety of events from corporate away days to weddings, and for two days each year, is home to one ofLondon’s largest free outdoor arts festivals.

Bordered at one end by the Thames, the Lawns are attractive, mid-sized outdoor spaces, each divided into four quadrants with a central fountain.

Measurements:King William Lawn 96m x 40mKing Charles Lawn 88m x 40m

GDIF, 2015 © Old Royal Naval College

Smaller-sized, off-shoot spaces suited to intimate outdoor events of 300-600 people, or as a base for activities in the wider area. Pepys Lawn offers access to the Old Brewery and the Visitor Centre, whilst Monument Gardens overlooks the iconicCutty Sarkand the Thames River Walk.

Measurements:Pepys Lawn 40m x 15mMonument Gardens 30m x 10mChapel Garden 30m x 10m

May Fayre, 2008 © John Zammit

The red brick and Portland stone King William Courtyard is festooned with shells, sea creatures and other details. An ornate lantern is the centrepiece of a cobbled courtyard, arranged to echo the pattern of the Union Jack.

The Queen Mary Courtyard is less ornate and is surfaced with flagstones.

Both Courtyards have steps leading onto the Colonnades.

Measurements:King William Courtyard 48m x 30mQueen Mary Couryard 50m x 40m

Get a breath of fresh air on the King William and Queen Mary Colonnades either side of Upper Grand Square. With detailed baroque ceilings and the site’s distinctive outdoor lanterns, these make exceptionally beautiful open air spaces. Available for hire along with the Painted Hall, Chapel, and Undercrofts, or on their own.

Measurements:Colonnades 100m x 4mCentral wide area 24m x 8m

Dance GB, English National Ballet © Annabel Moeller

As part of our outdoor hire offer, our iconic domes and buildings can be illuminated in a host of colours to mark special occasions, anniversaries and highlight causes.

Organisations and charities wishing to promote their causes by lighting up, projecting images onto walls or flying flags from the buildings and grounds of Old Royal Naval College must request permission from the Greenwich Foundation for the Old Royal Naval College.

If you would like to request the lighting up of the domes, apply via the form which can bedownloaded here. Please send forms directly toevents@ornc.org.uk

World Heritage Day, 2017 © Vickie Flores

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

© 2025 Old Royal Naval College. All rights reserved.

================================================================================
PAGE 19: Indoor spaces - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/venue-hire/our-spaces/

HEADINGS: Indoor spaces, Venue hire, Painted Hall, Admiral's House, Queen Mary Undercroft, Nelson Room Private Dining, The Chapel

CONTENT:
Our flagship space, Sir James Thornhill’s baroque masterpiece, Britain’s ‘Sistine Chapel’ thePainted Hallis considered the ‘finest dining hall in Europe’. It makes a prestigious and elegant venue for weddings, gala dinners, awards ceremonies and drinks receptions.

Our neoclassicalChapelprovides an exceptional setting for weddings, concerts and awards ceremonies.

A pair of arresting vaulted undercrofts, are available day and night, for hire alone or in conjunction with the Painted Hall or Chapel. Commissioned by Charles II as his new royal palace in 1660, The Admiral’s House is our oldest building available to be hired in its entirety, by floor, or by room.

Venue Hire starting from £17,000 for the Painted Hall, £6,650 for the Queen Mary Undercroft and £5,450 for the Admirals House.



The awe inspiring Painted Hall is available for evening hire and particularly suited to large gala dinners, awards dinners and drinks receptions.

Treat your guests to genuine wow factor when they are called to dinner and are treated to the big reveal of the epic baroque interior.

Find out more about hiring the Painted Hall

Commissioned by Charles II as his new royal palace in 1660, Admiral’s House is our oldest building, with views of the Thames and a regal yet intimate atmosphere.

Available for both the serious and the fun side of business, an excellent venue for high profile receptions and dinners or meetings, seminars, and conferences.

Find out more about hiring Admiral’s House

Situated within the same building as the Chapel, the Queen Mary Undercroft can be hired exclusively for both evening and daytime events, making it ideal for all manner of professional or corporate events and gatherings.

Hire the Queen Mary Undercroft and your guests can even try their hand at bowling in our genuine Victorian Skittle Alley!

Find out more about hiring the Undercroft

Experience our intimate dining room, the Nelson Room, located through the Painted Hall, with an imposing roof lantern, monumental stonework and marble floor.

Find out more about hiring the Nelson Room

Let your music soar in one of London’s most atmospheric concert venues. With its breathtaking neoclassical interior and outstanding acoustics, the Chapel has hosted concerts and events for centuries.

Seating 340 in the main nave and 100 in the galleries, the Chapel lends itself to a whole range of events

Find out more about hiring the Chapel

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

PAGE 20: Catering & trusted suppliers - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/venue-hire/catering-trusted-suppliers/

HEADINGS: Catering & trusted suppliers, Venue hire, Catering, Trusted suppliers, Venue hire, Indoor spaces, Corporate & private events

CONTENT:
We have hand-picked a range of exceptional businesses for our recommended supplier list. We have built long-lasting relationships with these companies and professionals, who never fail to impress with their expertise, acumen and panache. They will work tirelessly to ensure that their service is everything you could wish for on your event.



Enhance your occasion with superb catering from our award-winning partners,Company of Cooks. Whether you need a marvellous feast for a gala dinner, an energising working lunch, or your perfect wedding breakfast, you will be amazed by the quality of food, drinks, and service.

From sourcing local ingredients to creating the most visually stunning dishes, Company of Cooks work with local suppliers to source ingredients and create special details to make your event even more memorable. Our focus is always on you and ensuring your catering is exactly how you want it to be.

Due to the World Heritage nature of the site at the Old Royal Naval College, we have hand selected our suppliers to ensure the safety of our venue whilst also providing the great quality and service we are happy to recommend.

Our list for catering, production and floristry is set and we cannot approve any offlist supplier. If you do wish to bring your own suppliers outside of this selection, we request they come for a site visit with one of the team in advance of them being confirmed, to avoid any last minute changes or problems.

Corporate Suppliers ListSpeciality Catering Packages

We can cater for events, big or small, opulent or intimate – whatever you are planning, you will find the perfect venue to suit your occasion. Seated dinners, standing receptions, conferences, weddings, summer and Christmas parties alike.

Have a look at the beautiful spaces available to hire at Old Royal Naval College.

Hire a venue with the wow factor for your private event.

PAGE 21: Client testimonials - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/venue-hire/testimonials/

HEADINGS: Client testimonials, Venue hire

CONTENT:
The Painted Hall really must be the most fantastic venue In London, if not the UK. The entire event was faultless, with highly attentive and courteous staff being very much involved in ensuring all the guests were cared for in a professional manner. The meal was excellent, and was very well presented as well as being delicious. An outstanding venue and caterer.

From the moment our guests arrived from the boat, we knew this would be our most epic event yet. This venue is magnificent and we hope we can find another reason to host an event here soon!

We had our wedding at the Painted Hall shortly after it reopened after the conservation works. Words cannot do justice to how beautiful the venue is – absolutely stunning, may be even breathtaking! The food was delicious and we got a lot of compliments from guests on it. All around, just a fantastic experience.

The Painted Hall has been on my list of venues for years and years and it didn’t disappoint, made all the more special by working with people who so obviously love what they do in a space that is breathtaking!

A quick email to say thank you very much for your help with our AGM. The meeting and reception went really well and everyone was very complimentary about the location, service and food. Please also pass on a big thank you to the team that helped on the day. It was a real pleasure to host the AGM in such a wonderful setting.

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

PAGE 22: Learning - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/learning/

HEADINGS: Learning, FEES, Learning, Reception and key stage 1, Key stage 2, Key stage 3 and above, Special Educational Needs and Disabilities, English for Speakers of Other Languages, Community Groups, Black Women in Greenwich, Black Sailors, Writers, and Entrepreneurs of 18c Greenwich, Digital Learning, Support Us

CONTENT:
Take part in a facilitated session orcontact us as a self-led group.

Inspiring people with the history of the Old Royal Naval Collegeis at the heart of what we do.Our free year-round learning programme provides opportunities for people to discover something new every day.

Alongside a thriving primary and secondary school programme, we run regular tours and workshops for community groups, BSL and Audio-Described tours and a lively and varied programme of free activities for families.

Sharing our spaces and our stories withpeople of all agesmeans we can explore everything from Tudor beehives and Georgian architecture to drunken sailors and Arctic explorers.

Discover the history and artistic genius behindthemagnificent Painted Hall and Neoclassical Chapel on one of our regular tours. Explore the lives of the sailors who found refuge here after a life at sea and about the many monarchs who crossed at our gates in our school and family sessions.

Our bright and well-resourced learning rooms allow us to run workshops and discussion groups alongside tours of our expansive site.

In September 2022, our education programme was awardedthe highlyesteemedSandford Awardforheritage education.Learn more.

Our schools workshops are free for state schools with the exception of Tudor Study Day.

Fee-paying schools pay £200 per workshop. Workshops will be invoiced at the end of the half term that the session takes place in.

Explore our hands-on cross-curricular workshops for reception and Key Stage 1 inspired by the art, history and architecture of the Old Royal Naval College.

We have a range of hands-on, cross-curricular workshops for Key Stage 2.

Enjoy engaging learning activities for Key Stage 3, including an opportunity to sketch in the Painted Hall.If you would like to bring a key stage 4 or 5 group, we would be happy to arrange a visit. Please get in touch to arrange this.

We run an exciting programme of workshops for primary and secondary SEND schools in the summer and autumn terms linking to the history of our amazing site.

With our in-house ESOL expertise and tutor resources, a visit to the Old Royal Naval College is a rewarding experience for English language learners of all levels.

If you are interested in bringing your community group to the Old Royal Naval College for either a self-led or facilitated visit, please complete our booking enquiry form.

A workshop that uncovers the stories of three Black women that lived in Greenwich

This active inclusion writing workshop highlights the history of black free and enslaved people in the 18th century.

Browse our range of free short films and downloadable resources which are for schools to make use of in class.

As a charity, one of our aims is to educate the public by inspiring and engaging them in heritage and creativity. Your support is vital in helping us continue this work.

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

© 2025 Old Royal Naval College. All rights reserved.

PAGE 23: Reception and Key Stage 1 - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/learning/reception-key-stage-1/

HEADINGS: Reception and Key Stage 1, Contact Us, Learning, Tactile Tales, Pattern and Shape, Impossible Creatures, Local History: Lord Admiral Nelson’s Lying-in-State, Local History: The Great Fire of Greenwich

CONTENT:
We run a series of hands-on cross-curricular workshops for Early Years and Primary Schools inspired by the art, history and architecture of the Old Royal Naval College.

All our Reception & Key Stage 1 schools workshops are free to state schools. Fee-paying schools pay £200 per workshop. Workshops will be invoiced at the end of the half term that the session takes place in.

To book one of our workshops, please fill in ourBooking Enquiry Form. Please note: Enquiry forms must be submitted two months in advance of your preferred date.

For more information please call the Learning Team on 020 8269 4725.

This fun and engaging multi-sensory session uses our very special tactile rug to engage young children with a story involving characters from the Painted Hall.

This fun and engaging multi-sensory session uses our very special tactile rug to engage young children with a story involving characters from the Painted Hall.

This interactive session explores the maths behind the stunning architecture and decorative work of the Chapel.

This interactive session explores the maths behind the stunning architecture and decorative work of the Chapel.

PAGE 24: Key Stage 2 - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/learning/key-stage-2/

HEADINGS: Key Stage 2, Contact Us, Learning, Impossible Creatures, Pattern and Shape, Curator for a Day (Primary), Tudor Study Day, Myths and Masks, Painted Ceiling Investigators, A Local History Study: Life at Sea and the Royal Hospital, Local history Study: Greenwich at War*, Hidden Maps: Symbols and Meaning, Local History: Lord Admiral Nelson’s Lying-in-State, Greenwich Sailors from Near and Far

CONTENT:
We run a series of hands-on cross-curricular workshops for key stage 2 inspired by the art, history and architecture of the Old Royal Naval College.

All our Key Stage 2 schools workshops are free to state schools, except Tudor Study Day, which cost £200. Fee-paying schools pay £200 per workshop. Workshops will be invoiced at the end of the half term that the session takes place in.

To book one of our workshops, please fill in ourBooking Enquiry Form. Please note: Enquiry forms must be submitted two months in advance of your preferred date.

For more information please call the Learning Team on 020 8269 4725.

================================================================================
PAGE 26: Special Educational Needs and Disabilities - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/learning/special-educational-needs-and-disabilities/

HEADINGS: Special Educational Needs and Disabilities, Information, Contact Us, Learning

CONTENT:
We are pleased to offer free outreach visits to SEND schools and schools with SEND units. We offer the outreach mainly to East and South-East London Boroughs but please get in contact to find out how we may be able to help.

We currently offer the following workshops:

An engaging hands-on session developing the understanding of old and new with an emphasis on turn taking and social interaction. Students can use expressive language, sign, and song to communicate and interact with props when exploring how travel has changed for us today.

A sensory story of a sailor’s journey around the world. Students can interact with objects and improve communication, motor skills and confidence as they travel the globe from their classroom!

Our sessions run to suit your school timetable. Our earliest session can be offered from 11am-12pm and our latest session can be run from 1.30pm-2.30pm. Please state your preference when booking. Facilitators will arrive 30 minutes before session start to set up.

Sessions are offered to a maximum of 10 pupils per group per session.Please note the maximum we can offer are 2 sessions a day.

There is an accessible toilet available but sessions in the Painted Hall have some access restrictions. Please notify us of any access requirements, including vehicle access, when you are making your booking.See more about accessibility.

To book one of our workshops, please fill in ourBooking Enquiry Form. Please note: Enquiry forms must be submitted two months in advance of your preferred date.

For more information please call the Learning Team on 020 8269 4725.

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

© 2025 Old Royal Naval College. All rights reserved.

================================================================================
PAGE 27: English for Speakers of Other Languages - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/learning/english-for-speakers-of-other-languages/

HEADINGS: English for Speakers of Other Languages, Learning, ESOL Festive Workshop

CONTENT:
Our ESOL programme started in 2013 as part of a conservation project by the Heritage Lottery Fund. Since 2013 we have developed in-house ESOL expertise, pre- and post-visit resources and a range of bespoke sessions.

A visit to the Old Royal Naval College is a rewarding experience for ESOL groups. Students will develop and practice their English language skills in a new environment, socialise with others and explore Sir Christopher Wren’s riverside masterpiece. Visits can be tailored to the needs, level, age and interests of your group and we welcome ideas about how the programme can be developed.

Please do let us know if you want to bring a self-guided group to visit. An outreach talk at your centre/college may be possible on request.

To enquire about booking an ESOL visit, please completeour booking enquiry form, letting us know the ESOL levels, ages and needs of your learners.

For specific enquiries about access or other concerns for members of your group, please contact the Learning and Community Team administrator onlearning@ornc.organd we’ll reply as soon as possible.

Bring your ESOL students for an informal 2 hour session exploring our marvellous site and its rich history

Bring your ESOL students for an informal 2 hour session exploring our marvellous site and its rich history

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

================================================================================
PAGE 28: Black Sailors, Writers, and Entrepreneurs of 18c Greenwich - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/learning/black-sailors-writers-and-entrepreneurs-of-18c-greenwich/

HEADINGS: Black Sailors, Writers, and Entrepreneurs of 18c Greenwich, Learning

CONTENT:
Learn about the complexities faced by Black sailors, merchants, and writers as they passed through Greenwich. Explore themes of empire, trade, naval power, and monarchy as you consider the lives of the naval veterans who retired to this site after their service at sea.

Workshops take place in our Clore Learning Centre and include a tour of the Painted Hall. Activities are designed to help build creative confidence and activate the imagination using accessible creative writing tasks.

This offer is run by a professional educator-writer in partnership with our Community Outreach. It can be booked by school groups KS3+ as well as community groups of young people or adults. The day consists of morning and afternoon sessions with a 30 minute lunch break in between. Timings, depth of content, and skill levels can be adjusted per group.

If you would like to book a session, please fill in ourCommunity Workshop Enquiry Form.

Photo credits: Olaudah Equiano, aka Gustavus Vassa © Unknown Artist via Smithsonian National Portrait Gallery.

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

© 2025 Old Royal Naval College. All rights reserved.

PAGE 29: Digital Learning - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/learning/digital-learning/

HEADINGS: Digital Learning, Learning

CONTENT:
These resources were produced to fit the needs of Key Stage 2, but they may also be suited for Key Stage 1.

The workshop films and resources have been designed so that they can be used in one single session or alternatively built into lesson plans over a period of time to aid with retrieval practice.

This KS2 session and accompanying resources links directly to both the study of Ancient Greeks in History and Myths and Legends in Literacy. It also links to writing-composition in English and skills practice in art and design.

Myths and Masks resources

This KS2 black history session and accompanying resources links directly to the study of local history in History. It also links to writing-composition in English and geographical skills in Geography.

Where in the World? resources

Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

================================================================================
PAGE 30: Group and coach visits - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/plan-a-visit/group-and-coach-visits/

HEADINGS: Group and coach visits, Plan a visit, Group Benefits, Choice of Tours and Bespoke Offerings, Gin Tasting, Christmas Concerts, Travel Trade Partners, International Student Groups, Coach Operators, Explore what’s here, Private tours, How to get here

CONTENT:
Planning a group visit? We’re delighted to welcome groups of all sizes to the Old Royal Naval College. From guided tours and self-led visits to bespoke experiences, we offer a range of options to suit different interests, timings and budgets. Whether you’re organising a day out for a community group, society, or travel company, our team is here to help you create a memorable experience.

Whether your group is here for just a one-hour tour, a full day itinerary or somewhere in between, we can plan a programme just for you. We recommend that you allow a minimum of 1.5–2 hours for your visit.



Groups are welcome to join ourdaily scheduleof public tours, including our600 Years of History Touror our Film location tourWigs, Wedding, Powder and Palaces, as well asPainted Hall Talks.Access to tours is subject to availability.

We recommend that groups book a private tour with one of ouraward-winningexpert guides, at a time of the group’s choosing to guarantee availability.

Private tours benefit from the option of including whispering guide technology to ensure that all guests can hear clearly.

Learn about the story of Greenwich Gin and its connection to maritime exploration. Sample various award-winning gins as you’re guided through a range of botanicals and flavour profiles. Available on Fridays and Saturdays only.

Enjoy a festive concert in the Chapel delivered by the award-winning Trinity Laban Choir, with a chance to join in and sign along to some of your favourites. Visit includes entry to thePainted Halland theVisitor Centre.

Dates:1, 8 & 15 December 2025

The Old Royal Naval College is the perfect addition to a London programme.

We welcome trade enquires for both FIT and group visits, and are happy to create bespoke packages.

We welcome international student group visits, either as optional excursions or as part of a programme. Let us know of any language request at the time of booking as our guides can speak many languages. Moreover, our audio guide for the Painted Hall is also available in 7 languages.

Emailgroups@ornc.orgto book or learn more.

We are the only tourist attraction in Maritime Greenwich that has coach parking on-site.

Alongside booking your tickets, please pre-book your coach parking by completing theonline coach booking form.

Please note: Confirmed numbers and payment are requested 3 weeks prior to visit date.







Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Registered Charity No. 1062519.

© 2025 Old Royal Naval College. All rights reserved.

PAGE 31: Regency Afternoon Tea on the Colonnades - Old Royal Naval College
================================================================================
URL: https://ornc.org/whats-on/afternoon-tea-on-the-colonnades/

HEADINGS: Regency Afternoon Tea on the Colonnades, Film Tour: Wigs, Weddings, Powder and Palaces, Cinematic Sounds: Film Music Concert

CONTENT:
Sun 21 Sept | Various timesTickets: £65 (Adults), £30 (Children)Colonnades, Old Royal Naval College, London SE10 9NN

Be transported back to Regency-era London with an afternoon tea inspired byBridgerton.

Indulge in a splendid al-fresco afternoon tea experience amidst the Regency grandeur of the historic colonnades,where many scenes from the Netflix hit show have been filmed.

Enjoy a selection of delicate finger sandwiches, delicious homemade scones with clotted cream and jam, and exquisite cakes and sweet treats with aBridgertontwist. Choose from a wide selection of British tea specialistHope & Glory, created by their renowned Tea Sommelier and Master Blender.Alternatively, turn tea into a special celebration with chilled Prosecco orVeuve de Valmante French Sparkling. Vegan,vegetarianand gluten free options available. Please specify any dietary requirements when booking.

Tickets also include access to thePainted Hall,Chapel, and the opportunity tojoin a tourled by one of our expert guides.

The Regency Afternoon Teas will be held at 12.30pm, 1.30pm, 2.30pm and 3.30pm onSunday 21 September 2025.







A post shared by Old Royal Naval College (@oldroyalnavalcollege)



Step into the world of period drama and experience the UK’s most filmed heritage site like never before.

Step into the world of period drama and experience the UK’s most filmed heritage site like never before.

Join us for an evening of unforgettable film music in the stunning Chapel of St Peter & St Paul, in partnership with Docklands Sinfonia to celebrate 100 years of filming at the Old Royal Naval College.

Join us for an evening of unforgettable film music in the stunning Chapel of St Peter & St Paul, in partnership with Docklands Sinfonia to celebrate 100 years of filming at the Old Royal Naval College.
